< Text>
I have been living here with my family for a year now. The apartment is laid out well, and has a large kitchen and gorgeous quartz countertops. The bedrooms are on opposite sides of each other, and the master features a large closet with built in shelves- perfect for all my shoes! The washer and dryer is in-unit, the appliances are stainless steel, and the cozy living room has a cute little gas fireplace. Our patio is nice sized, and we get lots of hummingbirds.

Maria in the front office is super helpful, kind, and a true asset. She responds in a timely manner to any phone calls or emails, and cares about the residents. She helped me locate some missing packages during the holidays, and makes sure that my maintenance concerns are addressed in a timely manner. She is a Gem and one of a kind!

The reason for 4 stars instead of 5, is because not everyone is as helpful as Maria. I had let the office know for months that a sprinkler was broken all summer, which was causing flooding. It was not addressed timely, and I had to get corporate involved. The community water bill is divided between residents, and it was attracting mosquitoes. It also made it difficult to walk my dog when the grass was constantly over watered. There are homeless that live behind the ravine, which our family has personally called the police on multiple times. They are known to jump in the pool during the hot months, and have broken into a car, as well as the soda machine and mail boxes. I hope that a wall can be built, just as the homes on the opposite side of the ravine have- for safety.

Otherwise, there are lots of kids for my son to play with, a nice sized pool, a decent gym, and overall a nice place to live.<//Text>

115479670739355048223< /userid>
<review>Sometimes Sumo is a 3 star experience... Sometimes it's a 5. I'm not sure what accounts for the inconsistency, but it's a little strange.

The first three times I went, it was extremely good, and for a very reasonable price. The rolls were simple, but very well made and very robust. The spicy tuna in particular was excellent, with a bright red color that showed freshness and ample use of spices. The sashimi was mouthwatering and perfectly cut. Even the miso soup at Sumo is particularly great. My brother and I got out of Sumo for under $40 at dinner, and to put it mildly, we ate a ridiculous amount of high quality fish and appetizers.

But then I've been there twice where the experience was different. Despite the place being nearly empty, our server took about 10 minutes just to get us menus for some reason (not typical), and we got one water refill after we had already finished our meal (kind of pointless). I ordered the same spicy tuna roll, and it was completely different from my previous visits... It was a pale orange color, and was mostly rice. Not great. The California roll was also overburdened with rice and the surimi and Crab mix was grossly filled with a ton of mayo.

The price during lunch on a Wednesday was also somehow more than it was during dinner on a Saturday, even though the visits were just a few weeks apart. The staff wasn't as friendly either, and never asked us hoe our food was.

It's strange that the experiences were so totally different in a span of just a few weeks... But they were. I love Sumo, and have some great memories there with friends and family. I just wish they were more consistent.

Tips:
Sit at the bar. You get a lot more service there, and the chefs will even talk to you about your food. It's a nice experience.

Wednesdays offer extremely affordable saki bombs. If that's what you're into, I doubt there's a better deal anywhere else.

The spicy tuna roll is pretty cheap and is (usually) extremely good. It's the best I've had anywhere when it's done right.< /review>< response>
None<//response>

<rating>1</rating><userid>110094099451968294519</userid><Review>Me and my girlfriend went to taco Tuesday and the first thing we noticed was the chips were cold. In the past I remembered the chips being served warm because they were placed underneath a heat lamp. The salsa was unusually bland with absolutely no spice and my girlfriends margarita had very little to no alcohol with a small amount of salt on the rim. This was a huge disappointment because in the past their margarita's were flavorful with plenty of salt on the rim. At this point we were almost ready to leave, but we decided stay and order our usual hard shelled tacos with shredded beef and chicken. Then its gets worst because it took a long time to receive our order and when the tacos were served they were cold. They also lacked flavor, cheese, tomatoes, and the meat was filled with water, which made the tacos turn soggy.
